< review>
Solid sandwich place. Perfect for customization. Guy at the register walks you through your options to help you build your sandwich the first time. Some simple yes or no questions (bacon? avocado?) or some choices, like which kind of cheese or mustard. And there are a lot of options you can choose from. They run through all these choices on a computer and print out your order to make sure it's right, and it sounds like they store it for any future orders too. I wish more places were run like this.

Can be a little easy to miss going past. There is paid street parking on the street right out front, or a lot behind the nearby Safeway. The only seating around is the benches on the sidewalk along the street.</review>

<Resp>None< /Resp><username>Laci Hendricks< /username><pics>None</pics>< text>
WOW!!! These guys & gals are THE BEST!!

From Los Angeles, myself and 2 other girls were packed up and set to leave our campground that was about 30 miles away from Groveland, ON THE 4th of JULY. I started my heavily packed car and it sounds awful and would barely go until it died and wouldn't start again; I had JUST had it serviced a few days before the trip up to Yosemite. We hiked a mile to Evergreen Lodge who were kind and generous enough to let us use their computers and call a tow truck. We found Miller Brothers and called and explained the situation AND found out they are contracted with AAA. Within an hour Josh came and picked us up @ the comfy lodge, took all 3 of us back to the campground, loaded up the car and gave me great comfort the whole ride to the shop that all would be fine. They all made us feel like we were more like family than complete strangers. They gave us a diagnosis of a defective part, the brand new timing belt and let us know how long it would take, which unfortunately for us, fortunate for them, they had so many other cars to fix that it couldn't be fixed before the following week. They were SO honest and helpful; many small town shops I've dealt with in the past would have totally taken advantage of 3 destitute women and tried to rip them off. Not them...they're reputation around town as we explored Groveland was impeccable. Josh even took us into town to find a motel to crash at for the night. While we ate dinner and celebrated the holiday as best we could, we were assured by all the locals that my car was in good hands. I can't thank the mechanic Lee, his wife and cohort, Brittany...all of them actually, enough for their help and honesty for a smooth car trouble experience. It couldn't have been any better!!<//text>

< review>
Over the last several months of 2017 I was dealing with lower back, leg and hip pain. Things came to a head in January of 2018 when after a trip to Disneyland I was in considerable pain and within a couple of day after my trip I was barely able to walk or stand.

After allowing myself a moment to heal up I was referred to Dr. Tebbe by a family member. I made an appointment with him and saw him a few days later. Dr. Tebbe asked me a series of questions to get an idea of my activity and what I was doing leading up to my last major incident. He then proceeded to do a thorough examination and began to determine what my issues were. Ultimately he figured out a major part of my issue was that my right hip was out of alignment. Dr. Tebbe re-adjusted my hip and suddenly I started to feel like normal again. He also offered recommendations for managing this issue.

After my visit with Dr. Tebbe I am able to walk longer distances and have a more normal active life. Prior to seeing Dr. Tebbe I was limited in distance and mobility and dealing with pain and discomfort on a regular basis. With continued treatment from Dr. Tebbe I am able to have a higher quality of life that I honestly thought I had lost for good.

Thank you Dr. Tebbe for all that you do and in helping me be at my physical best!</review>

<Name>Lindsey Amanda</Name><Time>1544846623769< /Time><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
The junction is a place I visit often. Price Co foods is a decently priced grocery store that is convenient as it is close to home. The cigarette store is in the far corner. Wells Fargo is my bank, located right next to Starbucks. Then of course CVS for medicine, all kinds of things I tend to need while I'm there & who doesn't need to stop in at the Dollar store? I do! Famous footwear wear, Kohl's & TJMaxx are also visited frequently. I would rather hit up the junction for my shopping needs as it is so much more convenient, faster & friendlier than a trip to Walmart. Doesn't matter if I only need 1 item on my way home or a whole list of things, the junction is the place I stop. The junction also has other stores I didn't mention like a jewelry store,Jack in the box, Togo's, subway, a place to get nails done BBVA bank & a few more<//Review>
